El proceso de cifrado impide que los datos se filtren o bloqueen. \r\n\r\n− Por qué usar una VPN\r\nCon una VPN, no solo puede desbloquear servicios censurados o con restricciones geográficas, como Facebook, Pandora y Youtube, sino que, además, podrá navegar por Internet de forma anónima y con más privacidad y seguridad.\r\n\r\n- VPN frente a proxy\r\nTanto una VPN como un proxy pueden camuflar su identidad cambiando la ruta del tráfico de Internet y la IP. Sin embargo, un servidor proxy se basa por completo en el navegador y podría no ser compatible con determinadas páginas web que usan tecnología no basada en navegador. Por el contrario, un servicio de VPN cifra todo el tráfico y funciona con servicios basados en Internet. En resumen, una VPN proporciona más libertad, privacidad y seguridad al navegar por Internet.\r\n\r\n− ¿Por qué elegir la VPN de Hotspot Shield?\r\nLa VPN de Hotspot Shield es la marca de VPN de mayor confianza y ofrece un rendimiento óptimo en cuanto a velocidad, estabilidad y seguridad.  Hotspot Shield logra mantener la privacidad y seguridad en las actividades en línea del usuario, los sitios que visita, las búsquedas que realiza y su información de identificación personal. La VPN de Hotspot Shield ofrece las siguientes funciones básicas gratis:\r\n- Desbloqueo de cualquier sitio web o aplicación; acceda a contenidos con restricciones geográficas desde su dispositivo, esté donde esté.\r\n- Protección absoluta contra la ciberdelincuencia; el cifrado de datos de Hotspot Shield es tan seguros como el de los bancos y oculta su dirección IP de los intrusos.\r\n- Anonimato completo; oculte su dirección IP, identidad y ubicación de los sitios web y de los rastreadores de Internet.\r\n\r\n* Acerca de AnchorFree™\r\nAnchorFree es una empresa privada de capital de riesgo con sede en Silicon Valley. Cinebench scores are used by system administrators to help make purchase decisions, journalists to review hardware, hardware manufacturers to optimize their latest products, as well as computer owners to evaluate their individual system. \r\n\r\nImprovements to Cinebench Release 20 reflect the overall advancements to CPU and rendering technology in recent years, providing a more accurate measurement of Cinema 4D's ability to take advantage of multiple CPU cores and modern processor features available to the average user.\r\n\r\nCinebench R20 FAQs:\r\n\r\n•\tCinebench R20 uses a much larger and more complex test scene than R15 requiring about 8x the computational power needed to render it. The test also requires about 4x the memory. Therefore R15 and R20 results cannot be compared.\r\n\r\n•\tCinebench R20 and Cinema 4D R20 incorporate the latest rendering architectures, including integration of Intel’s Embree raytracing technology and advanced features on modern CPUs from AMD and Intel that allow users to render the same scene on the same hardware twice as fast as previously. \r\n\r\n•\tCinebench R20 provides improved benchmark accuracy for current and next generation CPUs to test if a machine runs stable on a high CPU load, if the cooling solution of a desktop or notebook is sufficient for longer running tasks to deliver the full potential of the CPU, and if a machine is able to handle demanding real-life 3D tasks.\r\n\r\n•\tCinebench R20 does not test GPU performance.\r\n\r\n•\tCinebench R20 will not launch on unsupported processors. On systems lacking sufficient RAM to load the test scene, a warning will be displayed and the CPU benchmark will not be executed.\r\n\r\n•\tBackground tasks can significantly influence measurement and create diverse results. It's always a good idea to shut down all running programs and disable any virus checking or disk indexing, but it's impossible to eliminate all background processes. Modern operating systems perform various background tasks that cannot or should not be disabled, even though they could have a minor influence on the results.\r\n\r\n•\tTest results can vary slightly because it's impossible to disable every background task of the operating system. These tasks are one factor that may have a slight influence on measurements. For instance, processors will reduce clock speed when running too hot to allow for cooling and prevent damage. With many modern processors the reverse is also true. They are able to overclock themselves when the temperature is low enough. So, a system freshly started in a relatively cool environment will typically run faster than the same system that has been performing benchmarks for several hours in a heated
